name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted May 11, 2024
msg:Nanjing Xuanwu Hotel 13th Floor Parent-Child Room Experience Review

Recently, I took my children to Nanjing and chose Xuanwu Hotel in the city center as our place of stay. It is particularly worth mentioning that we booked a parent-child room on the 13th floor. It not only has a superior geographical location, but also the room design is full of childlike fun and warmth, which brings us a different parent-child experience.

Location and environment

Xuanwu Hotel is located in the center of Nanjing, with convenient transportation around it. It can be easily reached by subway or bus. There are many attractions around it, and it is within walking distance to popular attractions such as Xuanwu Lake Park and Nanjing Museum, which is very suitable for family travel.

Room facilities

The facilities of the parent-child room are very complete. In addition to the regular bedding, TV, and independent bathroom, it is also specially equipped with children's beds, children's toys, and parent-child reading areas. These facilities greatly satisfy the curiosity of children, allowing them to play in the room. The decoration style in the room is mainly cartoon elements, with bright colors, giving people a lively and pleasant feeling.

Service experience

The service of Xuanwu Hotel is very thoughtful. From check-in to check-out, every detail makes people feel the warmth of home. The service staff at the front desk are warm and friendly, and patiently answer our questions. The room service staff will clean the room on time every day to keep the room tidy. In addition, the hotel also provides children's breakfast service, so that children can enjoy delicious breakfast during the trip.

Parent-child activities

In addition to the facilities in the room, Xuanwu Hotel also provides a wealth of parent-child activities. For example, in the outdoor area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe hotel, there are special children's play facilities where children can play to their heart's content. The hotel also regularly holds parent-child baking, parent-child painting and other activities, allowing us to enjoy food and art while also enhancing parent-child relationships.

Summary

Overall, the parent-child room on the 13th floor of Nanjing Xuanwu Hotel left a deep impression on us. Whether it is room facilities, service experience or parent-child activities, we feel the warmth and comfort of home. If you also plan to travel to Nanjing with your children, you might as well choose this place as your place to stay. I believe you will spend a happy parent-child time like me.

msg:The most satisfying thing about the Nanjing trip is the hotel. I will definitely choose this hotel when I come to Nanjing again in the future. It is the first choice for traveling with the elderly and children;
The service is the best in the overall Nanjing trip, very good, and the room type has been upgraded; there are two large and one small double-bed rooms, and the big bed is not crowded at all, and the baby can sleep comfortably in the middle; Oh, by the way, the air conditioning is very warm, and there is no fear of winter;

The location is excellent, it is right outside Exit 1 of Xuanwumen Metro Station. If you bring the elderly, you can choose to exit the barrier-free elevator opposite and then cross the road. If you come from Shanghai, you can go from Shanghai Railway Station to Nanjing Railway Station. Nanjing Station is only 2 stops away from Xuanwumen, the king; it is very convenient to get to any scenic spot, and you can walk to Xuanwu Lake Park. You can watch the sunrise every day from the sightseeing elevator If the room is a lake view room, you should be able to see the sunrise every day. I rely on the reflection of the bay window to judge the sunrise, and our two rooms can see the sunset;

Although the room is not big, it is clean, tidy and comfortable. The shower room in the bathroom is really big and has won unanimous praise. It can wash away daily fatigue. If you like a bathtub, you can also take a bath. The disposable utensils are also good and complete. Children's utensils are also provided; the waiter can be met at almost any time every day, with a high frequency, and will take the initiative to smile and serve. It is much better than other five-star hotels. It is truly an old five-star hotel that carries history and power;

For breakfast, it is highly recommended to eat at least once. The revolving restaurant with a lake view is really great The breakfast was a bit monotonous. We ate almost the same food for three days. But there was nothing good for breakfast outside Nanjing. For example, the area near the Presidential Palace was really terrible. I had to walk a lot to find a place to eat. I highly recommend eating a full breakfast and lunch. We usually eat a full breakfast and lunch casually, and order takeout from the hotel at night.

The sightseeing elevators are No. 4 and No. 5 elevators, and you don‚Äôt have to wait for a long time. There are three elevators, 123 and 123, which are very many. Overall, there is no problem at all. The room price plus two breakfasts is controlled at just over 600, which is the best value for money.

I would like to recommend a few more routes from the hotel. Bus No. 1 goes directly to Nanbao Park, and you can walk to Nanjing Yangtze River Bridge. Go to the glass plank bridge and the water circle to watch the sunset. You can walk to the Yangtze River and the Xiaguan train theme area, take a taxi back, it's leisurely, you can also add the Yuejiang Tower, but the tickets are a rip-off and the elevator costs money, so you can choose it yourself;

The overall tourism in Nanjing is very ugly, money is everywhere, the tickets are ridiculous, and if you have a broken leg, you have to take a taxi to the sightseeing bus, which is very unfriendly to the elderly. When I met the old Nanjing locals at Yuhuatai, they all went to Yuhang, and they cursed that Nanjing was not like this when they were young. Now I see that my hometown is complaining about the ugly appearance, so have a bottom line in your heart first, don't expect too much, this hotel is likely to be the happiest part of the trip, I wish you a good time
